 ' Night shift and frequent changes in it may increase the risk of heart disease in women slightly
 ek nae adhyayan main yah baat saamne ai he
 The study found that women who have been working on night shifts for more than ten years have a 15 to 18 percent higher risk of coronary heart disease (CHD)
 siechdi kii kai vajah hoti hai jaise dhumrapaan, asantulit aahaar, shaareerik shram kii kami or ucch body maas index
 The lead author of the study, Celine Vetter, from Bringham & Women's Hospital in the US, said in a statement, "during the research, we have seen that despite the control of these risk factors, changing night shifts carries the risk of CHD in women
 " Researchers had studied data from Nurses Health One and Nurses Health Two to find out the relationship between night shift and CHD, with a study of 2,40,000 female nurses over a period of 24 years

 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he) Narendra Keshav is currently a parliamentarian from the South Lok Sabha seat of Goa State, located on the west coast of India
 unhone saal 2014 ke loksabhaa chunaav main bhartiya janata party (BJP) ke tikat se pehali baar saansad kaa chunaav jeeta he
 Goa state with two Lok Sabha seats is very important politically
 yahaan par bhartiya janata party ek majboot party he
 In the religious text Mahabharata, Goa is mentioned as a country of cow grazers
 goa samudri taton or prakritik khubsuurati ke liye duniyabar main mashhoor he
 Located in the Konkan region of India, this state is full of Indian and foreign tourists
 yahaan ke logon kii aajeevika bhi paryaton par nirbhar he yani is sansadeey kshetra kii janata kii aay kaa jariya paryaton he
 Goa's per capita income is nearly two and a half times more than India's per capita income
 lihaaja isko bharat kaa sabase amir rajya kaha jaataa he
 The state of Goa was first a colony of Portugal, which was handed over to India by the Portuguese in 1961
 goa kshetrafal kii nazariye se bharat kaa sabase chota rajya he or jansankhya ke hisaab se iskaa sthaan chauthaa he
 The South Goa Parliamentary constituency is spread over an area of 1966 square kilometers
 iske tahat 5 taalluk aate hai
 Political Background: Apart from Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) in South Goa Parliamentary constituency, Congress Party, Nationalist Congress Party (NCP), United Goa Democratic Party (UGDP), United Goa Party (UGP) and Goa Forward Party (GFP) and Maharashtrawadi Gomantak Party ( MAG)
 is seat ko congress party kaa garh mana jaataa he
 There have been 13 Lok Sabha elections so far, of which the Congress party has won 8 times
 iske alaava is seat par bijepi ko 2 baar, ujidipi ko ek baar or ujeepi ko 2 baar jeet mili he
 The by-elections were also held in this seat in 2007, in which the Congress party won
 bhartiya janata party ke edwocket narendra keshav sawaikar yahaan se maujuuda saansad hai
 He is elected for the first time MP
 isse pehle saal 2009 ke loksabhaa chunaav main sawaikar ko congress party kii francisco sardinha ke haathon haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa tha
 In the year 2004 too, Congress won this seat
 agar abhi tak hue loksabhaa chunaavon par najar daalen, to ek baat saaf hoti he ki yahaan ke voter party ke naam par vot dete hai
 The social constituency of the South Goa seat is a Christian and Golden Hindu dominated seat in the south Goa parliamentary constituency
 yahaan ke log aajeevika ke liye paryaton, louh khanij or matsay paalan par nirbhar hai
 Tourists from different parts of India and the world arrive here to enjoy the beaches and natural beauty

 The state of Goa currently has a coalition government led by the Bharatiya Janata Party
 haalia goa vidhansabha chunaav main kisi bhi dal ko spasht bahumat nahin mila tha

 iske alaava teen nirdaleey vidhayak bhi jite

 manohar parrikar soobe main bijepi kaa bada cheharaa maane jate hai

 vartmaan main yahaan kii rajyapal mridula sinha hai
